<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луч</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">luč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́стый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучистый.html>лучи́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lučístyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лучи́стее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лучи́стей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> radiant, glowing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> radiant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">arising from radiation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>radially diverging, diverging from a point</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лучи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучиться.html>лучи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lučítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shine <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of light or a light source</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gleam with emotion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of eyes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to radiate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of emotions on one's face or in one's eyes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежность.html>не́жность</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучиться.html>лучи́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лице́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">néžnostʹ <b>lučílasʹ</b> v jevó licé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tenderness <b>radiated</b> on his face</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to radiate outwards <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of wrinkles around the eyes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лучи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">luk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучник.html>лу́чник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lúčnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучник.html>лу́чника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучник.html>лу́чники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучник.html>лу́чников</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lúčšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">superlative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoróšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>:
<ol><li>best</li></ol>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">э́тo <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мната</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>lúčšaja</b> kómnata.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is the best room.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Oн <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игрок.html>игро́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нды</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>lúčšij</b> igrók nášej komándy.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is the best player on our team.</span></div></dd></dl>
<ol><li>better</li></ol>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>lúčšij</b> variánt.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is a better choice.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жа</a> (3775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lýža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́ж</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжный.html>лы́жный</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжный.html>лы́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lýžnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ski

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжный.html>лы́жная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:база.html>ба́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lýžnaja</b> báza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ski pavilion; ski depot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лыжня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжня́</a> (20758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lýža</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ski</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжня́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lyžnjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжни́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ski track, trail left by a pair of skis, or one artificially created for the purpose of skiing on
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1989</b>,  Григорий Федосеев (Grigórij Fedoséjev),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:меченый.html>Ме́ченый</a> (Méčenyj, "The Marked One")</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=bQ_PAAAAQBAJamp;pg=PT207amp;dq=%22%D0%BB%D1%8B%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%8F%22">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́жу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впереди.html>впереди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взбить.html>взби́тый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:подходить.html>подхожу́</a> бли́же — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжня.html>лыжня́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:наклоняться.html>наклоня́юсь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ощупывать.html>ощу́пываю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>край</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыхлый.html>ры́хлый</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>прошёл</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́тились</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> две-три <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a> ра́ньше.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vížu vperedí vzbítyj sneg. Podxožú blíže — éto <b>lyžnjá</b>. Naklonjájusʹ, oščúpyvaju rukój kraj — on rýxlyj: čelovék tólʹko što prošól. My by vstrétilisʹ, pospéj ja vsevó na dve-tri minúty ránʹše.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I see in front of me ruffled snow. I come closer—it's a <b>ski trail</b>. I bend over and feel the edge with my hand—it's loose: someone had just come through. We would have met, if I had only been here two or three minutes sooner.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***лыко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ко</a> (16772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лꙑко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lyko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lyko</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*lúnˀka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lýko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́к</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лы́чный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bast (plant fiber)</li>
<li>yarn, rope, or geotextile made of bast fiber</li></ol>

***лысый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>лысый</a> (10859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">լոյս</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">loys</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>лы́сый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lýsyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лысе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:лысеть.html>лысе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bald, bald-headed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лысый.html>лы́сым</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:намного.html>намно́го</a> лу́чше.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Lýsym</b> tebé búdet namnógo lúčše.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It'll be much better for you to be <b>bald</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>лы́сый</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lĭgota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лёгкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljóxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lʹgóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́т</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:льнуть.html>льнуть</a> (26662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льнуть.html>льнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lʹnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прильнуть.html>прильну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cling <i>(to)</i>, to stick <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cultivate (someone), to fawn on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel drawn towards</li></ol>

***льстить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстить</a> (11179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">льстити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lĭstiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лестити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lestiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьstiti</i>, derived as if from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lьstь</i> (whence <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>лесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lʹstitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:польстить.html>польсти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flatter, to adulate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фотография.html>фотогра́фия</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льсти́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dánnaja fotográfija vam ne <b>lʹstit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this picture doesn't flatter you</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lʹstitʹ</b> sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flatter oneself (with)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́ждой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lʹstitʹ</b> sebjá nadéždoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flatter oneself with hope</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to flatter, to please</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A transitive use of this verb occurs in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льсти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́ждой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lʹstítʹ sebjá nadéždoj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flatter oneself with hope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***льстящий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:льстящий.html>льстя́щий</a> (11179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льстящий.html>льстя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lʹstjáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lʹstitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:льстить.html>льстя́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubóvʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обильный.html>оби́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимица.html>люби́мица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubímica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимица.html>люби́мицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимица.html>люби́мицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимица.html>люби́миц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимец.html>люби́мец</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчик</a> (21749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимец.html>люби́мец</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubímec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubímčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> favorite, pet; teacher's pet; blue-eyed boy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">particularly someone who is manipulative and preys on someone's sympathies to the detriment of others</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>лю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>би́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-люб-</b>; суффикс: <b>-им</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>
